# U-Boot

# Kernel
```bash


tee_otp read_mmr 10
tee_otp read_mmr 11
tee_otp lock_status 15
tee_otp lock 15 2

tee_otp read_mmr 4
tee_otp read_mmr 5
tee_otp write_mmr 4 0x0014975B
tee_otp write_mmr 5 0x000004E7


tee_otp lock_status 20
tee_otp lock_status 21
tee_otp read_mmr 20
tee_otp read_mmr 21

tee_otp write_mmr 20 0x0014975B
tee_otp write_mmr 21 0x000004E7
tee_otp write_mmr 20 0x200000


tee_otp write_mmr 26 0x0000000c
tee_otp write_mmr 27 0x00000001


root@AM62x:~# cat /tmp/mac_addr.txt
00:14:97:A3:B8:F3
00:14:97:A3:B8:F4



OTP MMR 26: 0x1497a3
OTP MMR 27: 0xb8f30000
OTP MMR 28: 0x1497a3
OTP MMR 29: 0xb8f40000

0x1497a3
0x1497ab
0x1497af
0x801497af

tee_otp read_mmr 26
tee_otp read_row 34
tee_otp write_row 34 0xE014 0x2000

tee_otp lock_status 34
tee_otp lock 34 4

tee_otp write_row 34 0xF014 0x1000
```


```bash
# 创建启动脚本
cat > /etc/init.d/optee << EOF
#!/bin/sh
### BEGIN INIT INFO
# Provides:          optee
# Required-Start:    $local_fs
# Required-Stop:     $local_fs
# Default-Start:     2 3 4 5
# Default-Stop:      0 1 6
# Short-Description: Start OP-TEE services
### END INIT INFO

case "$1" in
    start)
        echo "Starting OP-TEE services..."
        modprobe optee
        /usr/sbin/tee-supplicant -d
        ;;
    stop)
        echo "Stopping OP-TEE services..."
        killall tee-supplicant
        modprobe -r optee
        ;;
    *)
        echo "Usage: $0 {start|stop}"
        exit 1
        ;;
esac
exit 0
EOF

chmod +x /etc/init.d/optee
update-rc.d optee defaults



# 可以通过以下环境变量自定义编译
export CFG_TEE_CLIENT_LOG_LEVEL=2  # 日志级别
export CFG_TEE_CLIENT_LOAD_PATH=/lib  # 库加载路径
export CFG_TEE_FS_PARENT_PATH=/data/tee  # TEE 文件系统路径


# 在目标板上启动 tee-supplicant 时启用调试输出
/usr/sbin/tee-supplicant -d

# 检查系统日志
dmesg | grep -i tee

# 使用 strace 跟踪
strace /usr/bin/otp_keywriting read 0x123456


# 检查库依赖
ldd /usr/bin/otp_keywriting

# 检查设备节点
ls -l /dev/tee*

# 检查权限
chmod 666 /dev/tee*

# 检查 tee-supplicant 状态
ps aux | grep tee-supplicant


```

```bash


# 检查 tee 设备是否存在
ls -l /dev/tee*

# 如果设备不存在，加载驱动
sudo modprobe optee

# 读取 OTP
tee_otp read 0x123456

# 写入 OTP
./otp_keywriting write 0x123456 0xaabbccdd 0x11223344

# 锁定 OTP（例如：同时使用软锁和硬件写锁）
./otp_keywriting lock 0x123456 5   # 5 = 1(软锁) + 4(硬件写锁)

# 如果遇到库找不到的问题，更新库缓存
sudo ldconfig

# 检查 tee 设备权限
sudo chmod 666 /dev/tee*

# 检查日志
dmesg | grep -i tee

# 添加调试信息输出
export OPTEE_LOG_LEVEL=4

# 使用 strace 追踪系统调用
strace ./otp_keywriting read 0x123456

# 查看帮助
./otp_keywriting

# 读取示例（地址使用十六进制）
./otp_keywriting read 0x100

# 写入示例（所有值使用十六进制）
./otp_keywriting write 0x100 0x12345678 0x9abcdef0

# 锁定示例（锁定类型可组合）
./otp_keywriting lock 0x100 1  # 仅软锁
./otp_keywriting lock 0x100 3  # 软锁 + 硬件读锁
./otp_keywriting lock 0x100 7  # 所有锁定类型
```

```bash
tee_otp read 2
tee_otp write 2 0x1122 0x3344

ll usr/lib/libckteec.*
ll usr/lib/libseteec.*
ll usr/lib/libteec.*
ll usr/sbin/tee-supplicant


./compile.sh -p rpmsg
cp -r targetNFS/usr/bin/rpmsg_char_simple output/
sync

```

```
root@AM62x:/# ps |grep tee
 1360 root     /usr/sbin/tee-supplicant
 1361 root     [optee_bus_scan]
 1371 root     grep tee
root@AM62x:/#
```

```bash
tee_otp read_mmr 26
tee_otp read_mmr 27
tee_otp read_mmr 28
tee_otp read_mmr 29
```

```bash
tee_otp read_row 0
tee_otp read_row 1
tee_otp read_row 2
tee_otp read_row 3
tee_otp read_row 4
tee_otp read_row 5
tee_otp read_row 6
tee_otp read_row 7
tee_otp read_row 8
tee_otp read_row 9
tee_otp read_row 10
```


```bash
tee_otp write_mmr 15 0x88776655
tee_otp read_mmr 15
```

```txt
Usage:

  MMR Operations:
    - tee_otp read_mmr  <mmr_addr>
    - tee_otp write_mmr <mmr_addr> <value>

  Row Operations:
    - tee_otp read_row  <row_addr>
    - tee_otp write_row <row_addr> <value_low> <value_high>

  Locking Operations:
    - tee_otp lock <row_addr> <lock_type>
    - tee_otp lock_status <row_addr>

    Lock Type:
      - Combination of the following flags:
          1 - Soft lock
          2 - Hardware read lock
          4 - Hardware write lock

  Notes:
    - Ensure you have the necessary permissions to perform these operations.
    - mmr_addr address range is 0 to 31.
    - row_addr address range is 0 to 41.
```


## 注意事项
```bash
tee_otp write_mmr 20 0x0014975B

# 执行上面代码写入mmr 20 后，如果想用下面的命令修改mmr 20的某一个位，会报错

tee_otp write_mmr 20 0x2800000

# 单独修改某个bit时，需要用 write_row 命令
tee_otp write_row 34 0xE014 0x2000
tee_otp write_row 34 0xF014 0x1000
```
